</body></html>Service Overview

AI debt collection service uses voice agents for reminders and negotiations, cutting costs 90% vs. humans (AI: $0.07-0.50/min; human: $0.75-1.25/min) while ensuring FDCPA/Regulation F compliance via scripted Mini-Miranda and 7-in-7 rules. Targets financial institutions with high delinquency volumes, focusing on early-stage/low-balance debts for 20-30% recovery gains.


Regulatory Compliance
Target Guatemala/Latin America first: Review Sugef (Superintendencia de Bancos) rules on automated calls; secure borrower consent for AI voices akin to TCPA. For US clients: Hard-code FDCPA disclosures, frequency caps, and hallucination guards (RAG for offers); audit 100% calls. Action: Consult local lawyer ($500-1k) today; build consent flags in client CRMs.


Technical Roadmap
Week 1: MVP Build (MacBook Pro)

Stack: Retell.ai/Vodex for voice ($0.07-0.50/min), OpenAI GPT-4o for LLM, Twilio for telephony, Stripe for payments.



Code prompt script: RPC verify  Mini-Miranda  Negotiate (PTP/settlement within bands)  Escalate humans  Real-time CRM API sync.

Deploy: Vercel/AWS; test 100 red-team calls for compliance.

Week 2-3: Pilot

Integrate client data (CSV delinquent lists); run 1k simulated calls.

Metrics: Answer rate >30%, PTP >20%, cost/debt <10%.


Week 4+: Scale

Add ML prioritization (Python scikit-learn on payment history).


Hybrid: AI Tier 1, human Tier 2.

Go-to-Market for Client
Immediate (48h): Pitch Potential Client

Demo MVP video (record 5 sample calls).

Proposal: $5k setup + $0.20/call or 10% recovery share; ROI: 2x liquidation, 50% cost cut.



Contract: 30-day pilot on 10k accounts.

Acquire More (Week 2+):

LinkedIn/Upwork: Post "AI Collections: 30% Recovery Boost, Compliant" targeting Guatemala banks (e.g., BAC, Banrural).


Price tiers: $2k/mo starter (5k calls), $10k/mo enterprise.


Win strategy: Free audit of their DPD rates + custom ROI calc.

Monetization & Risks
Aspect	Action	Projected Revenue
Pilot Client	Close $10k/mo post-30 days	$120k/yr
5 FI Clients (6 mo)	Upwork bids + LinkedIn cold outreach	$600k/yr
Scale	White-label via Vercel	$2M/yr
Risks: Yale study shows 1% lower repayment vs. humansmitigate with hybrid. Hallucinations: Temp=0, RAG only. Start small, iterate on metrics.


Craft a comprehensive, detailed, and clearly explained, verbose, SSD, to complete MVP Build from scratch.
System Architecture
Single-page dashboard (SSD) deploys a compliant AI debt collection voice agent MVP. Core flow: Upload CSV delinquents  Queue outbound calls via Twilio  Retell AI agent handles interaction (RPC, Mini-Miranda, PTP negotiation)  Stripe payment or CRM webhook  Log transcripts. Runs on Vercel (frontend/backend), AWS Lambda optional for scale. Latency <800ms; 100% compliance via RAG-grounded prompts.



Tech stack ensures Guatemala/US compliance: No calls outside 8AM-9PM local; consent check; dispute escalation. Expected: 20% PTP rate, $0.20/call cost.


Prerequisites & Setup
Install on MacBook Pro M1:

text
brew install node python3
npm create vite@latest debt-ai-mvp -- --template react-ts
cd debt-ai-mvp
npm i @retell/sdk stripe twilio openai axios dotenv zod csv-parser
pip install pandas openai twilio stripe
Accounts: Retell.ai (free tier), Twilio ($20 credit), Stripe test, OpenAI API key.



Env vars (.env): RETELL_API_KEY, TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID, TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN, TWILIO_PHONE, OPENAI_API_KEY, STRIPE_KEY.

Buy Twilio number (Guatemala/US); SIP trunk to Retell per tutorial.


Action: Run npm run dev; deploy vercel --prod.

Frontend: React Dashboard
Vite + React + Tailwind (add via npm i tailwindcss postcss autoprefixer). Single page: Upload CSV  View queue/logs  Metrics table.

App.tsx (full verbose code):

tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import Papa from 'papaparse';
import axios from 'axios';
import { z } from 'zod';

const DebtSchema = z.object({
  phone: z.string().min(10),
  name: z.string(),
  amount: z.number(),
  due_date: z.string(),
  consent: z.boolean().default(true), // Guatemala/Sugef check
});

interface DebtRecord {
  phone: string;
  name: string;
  amount: number;
  due_date: string;
  id?: string;
}

const App: React.FC = () => {
  const [records, setRecords] = useState<DebtRecord[]>([]);
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleFileUpload = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file) return;
    Papa.parse(file, {
      header: true,
      complete: (results: any) => {
        const parsed = results.data.map((row: any) => ({
          phone: row.phone,
          name: row.name,
          amount: parseFloat(row.amount),
          due_date: row.due_date,
        }));
        const validated = z.array(DebtSchema).safeParse(parsed);
        if (validated.success) setRecords(validated.data);
      },
    });
  };

  const queueCalls = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await axios.post('/api/queue-calls', { records });
      setLogs(prev => [...prev, `Queued ${res.data.queued} calls`]);
    } catch (err) {
      setLogs(prev => [...prev, `Error: ${err}`]);
    }
    setLoading(false);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchLogs = async () => {
      const res = await axios.get('/api/logs');
      setLogs(res.data);
    };
    fetchLogs();
    const interval = setInterval(fetchLogs, 5000);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="p-8 max-w-4xl mx-auto">
      <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-8">AI Debt Collection MVP</h1>
      <input type="file" accept=".csv" onChange={handleFileUpload} className="mb-4 p-2 border" />
      <button onClick={queueCalls} disabled={loading || !records.length} className="bg-blue-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded">
        {loading ? 'Queueing...' : `Queue ${records.length} Calls`}
      </button>
      <div className="mt-8">
        <h2 className="text-2xl mb-4">Records ({records.length})</h2>
        <table className="w-full border-collapse border">
          <thead><tr><th className="border p-2">Phone</th><th>Name</th><th>Amount</th><th>Due</th></tr></thead>
          <tbody>{records.map((r, i) => (
            <tr key={i}><td className="border p-2">{r.phone}</td><td>{r.name}</td><td>${r.amount}</td><td>{r.due_date}</td></tr>
          ))}</tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
      <div className="mt-8">
        <h2 className="text-2xl mb-4">Call Logs</h2>
        <ul>{logs.map((log, i) => <li key={i} className="mb-2 p-2 bg-gray-100">{log}</li>)}</ul>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;
Action: Tailwind config npx tailwindcss init; test upload sample CSV.

Backend: API Routes (Vercel Serverless)
api/queue-calls.ts & api/logs.ts. Node.js + Retell SDK. Use cron/queue for calls (upstash-kafka free tier optional).

api/queue-calls.ts (verbose):

ts
import { NextApiRequest, NextApiResponse } from 'next';
import { RetellAgentConfig, Retell } from 'retell-sdk';
import OpenAI from 'openai';
import Twilio from 'twilio';
import Stripe from 'stripe';

const retell = new Retell(process.env.RETELL_API_KEY!);
const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY });
const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_KEY!, { apiVersion: '2024-06-20' });
const twilioClient = Twilio(process.env.TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID!, process.env.TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN!);

const COMPLIANT_PROMPT = `
You are a compliant AI debt collector for [CLIENT_NAME]. Rules:
1. START EVERY CALL: "Hello, this is an AI assistant from [CLIENT_NAME] Debt Recovery. This call is an attempt to collect a debt. Am I speaking with {NAME}?" (Mini-Miranda/FDCPA).
2. Verify: Ask DOB last 4 SSN if needed for RPC.
3. If no consent/dispute: "Noted, we'll update records. Goodbye." Hang up.
4. Negotiate: Offer full pay, 50% settle min ${amount*0.5}, or PTP plan. Use Stripe link.
5. Escalation: Disputes/hardship  "Transferring to human." (webhook).
6. End: Confirm next steps, log.
7. Empathetic, no threats. Local time check: 8AM-9PM.
Context: Debt {amount} due {due_date}. Phone {phone}.
`;

export default async function handler(req: NextApiRequest, res: NextApiResponse) {
  if (req.method !== 'POST') return res.status(405).end();
  const { records } = req.body;

  let queued = 0;
  for (const rec of records) {
    // Create agent
    const agentConfig: RetellAgentConfig = {
      agentId: await createAgent(rec), // Func below
      fromNumber: process.env.TWILIO_PHONE!,
      toNumber: rec.phone,
      metadata: { amount: rec.amount, name: rec.name, due_date: rec.due_date },
    };

    // Queue outbound call
    const callId = await retell.startCall(agentConfig);
    // Log to DB (Vercel Postgres free)
    await logCall(callId, rec);
    queued++;
  }
  res.json({ queued });
}

async function createAgent(rec: any) {
  const completion = await openai.chat.completions.create({
    model: 'gpt-4o-mini',
    messages: [{ role: 'system', content: COMPLIANT_PROMPT.replace('{NAME}', rec.name).replace('{amount}', rec.amount.toString()).replace('{due_date}', rec.due_date).replace('{phone}', rec.phone) }],
  });
  const agent = await retell.createAgent({
    name: `debt-agent-${rec.phone}`,
    llmWebsocketUrl: `wss://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions?model=gpt-4o-mini`, // Custom via proxy if needed
    voice: 'jennifer', // Natural female
    instructions: completion.choices[0].message.content!,
    customFunctions: [ // Tools
      {
        name: 'process_payment',
        description: 'Generate Stripe link',
        parameters: { type: 'object', properties: { amount: { type: 'number' } } },
        execute: async (params: any) => {
          const paymentLink = await stripe.paymentLinks.create({ line_items: [{ price_data: { currency: 'usd', product_data: { name: 'Debt Payment' }, unit_amount: params.amount * 100 } }] });
          return { url: paymentLink.url };
        },
      },
      {
        name: 'escalate_human',
        description: 'Escalate to human',
        parameters: {},
        execute: async () => { /* Twilio warm transfer */ return { status: 'escalated' }; },
      },
    ],
  });
  return agent.agentId;
}

async function logCall(callId: string, rec: any) {
  // Vercel Postgres or JSON file
  console.log(`Call ${callId} for ${rec.phone}`);
}
api/logs.ts: Fetch Postgres/Supabase logs.

Action: npm i retell-sdk openai twilio stripe; SIP config Twilio  Retell.

- Close: "Thanks, expect confirmation SMS."

Define the MVP scope and core user flows for this product

AI-Debt-Collection-and-Payment-Reminders.pdf
MVP scope focuses on early-stage debt reminders for financial institutions in Guatemala/US, delivering 20-30% PTP uplift at $0.20/call via compliant voice AI. Excludes late-stage negotiation, analytics dashboard; prioritizes compliance (Mini-Miranda, consent, 7-in-7) and real-time payment capture for 1k accounts pilot.


MVP Features
CSV upload: Delinquent accounts (phone, name, amount, due_date, consent_flag).

Outbound voice calls: Retell.ai/Twilio agent with barge-in, low-latency LLM.

Compliance engine: Hard-coded FDCPA/Sugef scripts, time-zone scheduling, suppression lists.

Payment integration: Stripe links for full/PTP/settle (50% min).

Logging: Transcripts, outcomes (PTP/secured/escalated) to Vercel Postgres.

Metrics: Basic dashboard (call success 30%+, PTP 20% target).



Non-features: Human escalation, ML prioritization, inbound SMS, multi-language (add post-MVP).

Core User Flows
Financial Institution Admin Flow

Login dashboard  Upload CSV (100-1k records, validated Zod schema).

Review/queue calls  Confirm consent scrub (DNC/bankruptcy check via API).

Monitor real-time logs/table: Call ID | Phone | Status (ringing/answered/PTP) | Transcript snippet.

Download report: CSV outcomes, Stripe payments linked.

Debtor Flow (Voice Call)

Ring (8AM-9PM local)  Answer  AI: "Hello [NAME], AI from [BANK]. Attempt to collect debt. Confirm?"

RPC verify (optional DOB/SSN4).

Pitch: "${AMOUNT} due ${DATE}. Pay full/settle/PTP?"

Interact: Empathetic negotiation  Stripe URL SMS'd/voiced.

Close/objection: "Stop?"  Suppress. Dispute  "Noted, human follow-up."

Admin Metrics View

Metric	Target	Source
Answer Rate	>30%	Logs
PTP Secured	20%	Stripe webhooks
Avg Handle Time	<5min	Retell
Compliance Score	100%	LLM audit transcripts
Success Criteria
Pilot: 1k calls, 200 PTP ($ avg 100/debt = $20k collected), zero compliance flags. ROI demo for client close. Scale gates: 80% uptime, <1% hallucination (red-team verified).



List the technical stack and why each component is chosen
Technical Stack
MVP stack optimized for rapid deployment on MacBook Pro M1, low cost (<$50/week1), compliance, and scale to 10k calls/mo. Leverages your JS/Python/AWS/Vercel expertise; pay-per-use avoids upfront infra.


Component	Version/Tool	Why Chosen
Frontend	React + Vite + Tailwind CSS + Zod	Fast SPA dashboard (CSV upload/logs); Vite hot-reload for dev speed; Tailwind for brutal UI; Zod validates debt CSVs (phone/amount/consent). Your full-stack JS fit. Deploy Vercel 1-click.
Backend/API	Node.js + Vercel Serverless Functions	Serverless scales auto (0 to 1k calls); no ops. Handles queue-calls/logs; integrates SDKs seamlessly. Free tier covers MVP.
Voice AI Agent	Retell.ai SDK (GPT-4o-mini integration)	Low-latency (<800ms) barge-in voice; compliant prompts; debt-specific tutorials/examples. $0.07-0.50/min; custom functions (payment/escalate). Proven collections (Skit.ai alt).

Telephony	Twilio Programmable Voice + SIP Trunk	Reliable outbound (Guatemala/US numbers); SIP to Retell (free setup video). Consent/DNC scrub APIs. $0.01/min + $1/mo number. Battle-tested compliance.
LLM/Prompts	OpenAI GPT-4o-mini + RAG grounding	Empathetic negotiation; hallucination-proof (temp=0.1, tool-calling). Grounds FDCPA scripts/PDF data. Cheap ($0.15/1M tokens); your AI certs.
Payments	Stripe Payment Links	Real-time tokenized links (voice/SMS); PCI-compliant (AI can't steal cards). Auto-ledger webhooks to client CRM. Test mode Day1.
Data/Storage	Vercel Postgres (free tier) + PapaParse	Logs/transcripts/outcomes; query metrics. CSV ingest simple. Scale to Supabase later.
Queue/Scheduling	Vercel Cron + Timezone check (luxon lib)	Batch calls (8AM-9PM local); 7-in-7 enforcement. Add BullMQ post-MVP.
Deployment/Monitor	Vercel + GitHub	1-min deploys; env secrets; analytics. Your Vercel pref; AWS migrate for prod scale.
Testing/Utils	Playwright (E2E) + Python scripts	Red-team calls (dispute/pay/stop); compliance LLM grader. Pandas for CSV sims.
Rationale Summary
Cost/ROI: 90% cheaper than humans; stack totals $0.20/call.



Compliance: Deterministic scripts, audit trails beat humans 100%.



Speed: Week1 MVP; your stack (JS/Python/Vercel).

Risks Mitigated: Open-source alts ready (e.g., Bland.ai if Retell limits).
